Current Commentary

The Rise and Fall of the Two Major Opposing Forces in Europe

— Xing

The arms race and alliance diplomacy are the most important causes of international war. In recent days, the arms race and secret diplomacy in Europe have been proceeding with such speed and danger that they are unprecedented in European history. Italy is deploying troops in Southern Europe, boldly pursuing its plan for the Third Roman Empire. Germany is increasing its troops by more than one million, and in an instant, it can rampage across Europe and realize its ideal of the Third Reich. The Soviet Union is reducing the age of military service, France is striving to stockpile arms, and Britain is actively building ships. Between the Danube and the Rhine, small countries are scattered like stars, and military camps and fortresses are also springing up like bamboo shoots after a rain. However, the arms race, without the support of alliance diplomacy, would not immediately erupt. Now, the two major camps in Europe are pitted against each other. One, centered on France and the Soviet Union, and the other, led by Germany and Italy, are pursuing their diplomatic work with the utmost barefacedness. The activities in Spain are aside. In Poland, Romania, and Czechoslovakia, there are politicians who use their skills of alliances and conspiracies. The transformation from diplomatic war to bloody war is only a hair's breadth away.

Before the First World War, the protagonists of the Triple Alliance and the Triple Entente also constituted the countries of today's fascist front and anti-fascist front. Since the establishment of the German-Austrian alliance, the Italian-Austrian-Hungarian group has been integrated with Germany. After the front was arranged properly, it engaged in external development. In the west, it incited the civil strife in Spain to oppress France at the foot of the Pyrenees Mountains and threaten Britain between the Straits of Gibraltar. Since the fall of Irún, the fascist forces in Spain have had the possibility of seizing power. This is the success of the German-Italian front. On the eastern front, Romania has always been a friend of France. The former Foreign Minister Titulescu was the leader of the pro-French faction. The strong unity of Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, and Romania, and the peace of the Danube River Basin for more than ten years, were mostly due to his efforts. Now, as a result of the activities of the National Socialist Party in the Balkans and Germany's economic appeal, the cabinet was reorganized and Titulescu was dismissed. Romania, under one-party dictatorship, has a great tendency to turn to the German-Italian front. This is another success of the fascist side. Other events, such as the restlessness of the German Party in Czechoslovakia and the pro-German tendencies of the Regent of Hungary, all prove that the fascist forces in Central Europe are developing to the southeast. The Balkans has once again become a battlefield for Europe.

On the French-Soviet front, development has also been rapid. Most of the countries of the League of Nations are sympathetic to this front, and Poland's pro-French stance is certainly a success of French-Soviet diplomacy. At a time when the National Socialist Party is rampant in Danzig and Silesia, Poland, in order to secure itself, abandoned Germany and turned to France and the Soviet Union, which is also appropriate. French-Soviet diplomacy lost in the Balkans and gained in Poland. Although the gains and losses can be offset slightly, fascist diplomacy is extremely aggressive. Even to maintain its existing power, France and the Soviet Union must prepare for a major conflict. Commentators often say that armed peace can avoid a major war for a while, because the two sides are evenly matched, and neither side is willing to be in the position of launching a war. This observation can be applied to the international situation before the First World War, which is very different from the current situation. Today's Germany and Italy have a heart to break the status quo. It cannot be compared with 1914, and under the public advocacy of war and the promotion of aggression, armed peace has no possibility of existence.

Hebei-Chahar Inspectorate General Office; Eight Sub-Offices Being Established; Request Instructions from Ministry on Collection Rights and Limits

(Tianjin) The Hebei-Chahar General Inspection Office's regulations and tax collection rules have not yet been approved by the Hebei-Chahar Council. The office plans to start releasing private goods next week and collect inspection fees. Eight sub-offices, including Pingbao and Zhang, are being prepared for establishment. Each office will have one director and several inspectors to assist the customs in combating smuggling. The total operating expenses of the general office are 5,000 yuan per month. Since the 10th, many smugglers have gone to the office to apply for inspection. Regarding customs anti-smuggling and the collection rights and limits of the Hebei-Chahar Inspection Office, the Hebei-Chahar Council ordered Ge Dingyuan, Sun Weidong, Guo Zhihan, Deng Zhexu, etc., to negotiate in Peiping, and also telegraphed the Ministry of Finance for instructions to avoid conflicts and double taxation. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

(Tianjin) The workers and soldiers of the Qikou Cangyan Maritime Defense Inspection Office reported to Tianjin on the 10th. The person in charge of the Hebei-Chahar General Inspection Office still denies that the office's collection of inspection fees conflicts with customs anti-smuggling. After the collection of fees for private goods, the market price can also be discounted. Various trading companies have now received notices from the office to report and inspect goods. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

(Peiping) Now that the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee has established the Consumption Tax General Inspection Office in Tianjin yesterday, North China now has two tax collection agencies, one responsible to the local authorities and one responsible to the central government. Observers are now closely watching whether the customs authorities can confiscate the private goods for which the General Inspection Office has already collected consumption tax. Wang Hong'en, the director of the General Inspection Office, has promised that private goods that have already paid consumption tax can be freely transported to Hebei and Chahar for sale. However, according to news from Dagu, the customs authorities have stated that the establishment of the General Inspection Office has nothing to do with the anti-smuggling team established by the National Government, and the team will continue to serve as usual. Wang went to Qikou yesterday and established a new tax collection agency there, and organized a patrol team in Tianjin to investigate and prevent private goods that have not paid the new tax from being transported to Hebei. According to reliable Chinese sources, representatives of 20 stores selling private goods have now registered at the General Inspection Office, and 200,000 bags of sugar, among other private goods stored in Tianjin, will be taxed and put on the market. Whether the customs authorities can stop the sale of these goods is a question that everyone is asking each other today. Yesterday, news came from Nanjing that the Ministry of Finance has decided not to recognize this new tax. Whether its attitude will be effective will be seen in the coming days. (Reuters Telegram, 10th)

Hebei-Chahar Establishes Inspection Office; Kong Ling Another Plan; Establishing an Office and Collecting Taxes Hinders the Integrity of Customs Duties

(Nanjing) The Hebei-Chahar authorities sent another telegram to Finance Minister Kong regarding the establishment of the Hebei-Chahar Inspection Office, still stating that the establishment of the office is only to assist the customs in anti-smuggling and to prevent private goods that have already landed from being arbitrarily sold in the interior, so as not to conflict with the customs' authority. The outside world's transmission of the facts is too extreme. The telegram did not mention the collection of taxes on private goods. It is heard that Finance Minister Kong believes that the Hebei-Chahar authorities' intention to assist in anti-smuggling is very good, but if they truly establish an office to collect taxes, it will ultimately hinder the integrity of customs duties. He is now based on this principle and ordering the competent authorities to formulate another proper plan. He telegraphed the Hebei-Chahar authorities for inspection on the 10th. (Central News Agency Telegram, 10th)

Japanese People Plan to Invest in North China to Develop Cotton and Wool Industry

(Tianjin) The Japanese Ministry of Colonial Affairs plans to use a large sum of 1.52 million yuan to develop cotton production, improve wool, and control the cotton and wool industry in North China. This year, it will first allocate 200,000 yuan for two types of investigation fees. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

Central Government Decides to Support Hu Hanmin's Descendants

(Nanjing) The central government is giving preferential treatment to Hu Hanmin and has decided to support his descendants. Hu has no sons. The interpretation of "descendants" is based on direct bloodlines. (Special Dispatch, 10th)

Page 7

League of Nations General Assembly Scheduled to Hold Regular Meeting; Forecast of the Situation of Council Seat Allocation

(Geneva) China had previously requested the League of Nations Council for a quasi-permanent council seat. The Council approved it in May of last year and submitted it to the League of Nations General Assembly for review. At the General Assembly this month, it may approve the Council's proposal to establish a quasi-permanent council seat for China. In addition, the terms of the three current non-permanent council seats, namely Argentina, Australia, and Denmark, will expire this year. The General Assembly will hold elections to replace them. Approximately, the successor to Argentina will be either Colombia or Bolivia, the successor to Australia will be New Zealand, and the successor to Denmark will be Sweden. Also, the Council temporarily added a non-permanent council seat in 1933 for Portugal. Now that Portugal's term has expired, if the country is not re-elected, Latvia will succeed it. (Havas Telegram, 9th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations General Assembly is scheduled to hold a regular meeting on the 21st of this month. The Spanish government will send a delegation to attend at that time. The candidates are Foreign Minister Terbalut, former Foreign Minister Teros Rivo, and Catholic Conservative Party member Galadot, with Terbalut as the chief representative. (Havas Telegram, 10th)

(Geneva) The Economic Committee of the League of Nations met this afternoon and advocated convening an international conference with the participation of the United States, Germany, Italy, Britain, France, and other countries to discuss and resolve the economic panic, and to take stabilizing currencies, eliminating commercial restrictions, and the settlement system as the themes of discussion. (Havas Telegram, 9th)

Locarno Conference

(London) According to reliable news today, Britain has now scheduled to convene the Locarno Conference on October 19 and has invited France, Italy, Germany, and Belgium to send representatives to attend in order to negotiate a new Locarno Treaty. (Guomin Telegram, 9th)

United States Prepares to Implement Large Battleship and Cannon Policy; Believes Japan's Increase in Submarines Violates Treaty; British and American Representatives Discuss Response

(Washington) Secretary of the Navy Swanson announced today that a plan to build two new battleships has been drafted and may be equipped with 16-inch or larger cannons, but this will depend on whether Britain and Japan can abide by the restrictions of the New London Treaty. Swanson also stated that it is best to use 20-inch cannons, but naval experts have expressed doubts about this. The Navy Department is now waiting for President Roosevelt's order to begin laying the keels of the two battleships. Swanson also said that next year's naval exercise will be held in the waters off Hawaii and the North Pacific. (Guomin Telegram, 9th)

(Washington) US Chief of Naval Tactics, Admiral Stanley, told reporters today that if Japan does not agree to the 14-inch gun proposal by April 1, 1937, then the armaments of the two battleships to be built by the United States next year will be "sky is the limit." Secretary of the Navy Swanson also attended the meeting, his first since recovering from illness. It is said that Japan's suggestion to retain 15,598 tons of submarines exceeding their age violates the London Naval Treaty. The United States does not want to take any countermeasures before it is certain how Japan will proceed with this matter. The Secretary of the Navy opposes the establishment of a US naval detachment stationed in Europe, as this move would involve the United States in European political events. (Reuters Telegram, 9th)

(London) British and American representatives discussed today what policy the two countries should take regarding Japan's expansion of submarine tonnage beyond the limits of the London Treaty. The British Embassy in the United States sent a copy of the Japanese note to the United States last week to solicit the views of the United States. On Monday of this week, Johnson, the secretary of the American Embassy here, held further discussions with British naval expert Holmes. It is reported that the United States believes that Japan's decision is tantamount to invoking the "Escalator Clause," so the United States also has the right to take similar actions, meaning that the United States has also decided to increase submarine tonnage. (Guomin Telegram, 9th)

Soviet Air Force Transport Sets World Record: 18 Cannons, Over 100 Machine Guns, and 1,200 Soldiers Transported Behind Enemy Lines in 8 Minutes

(Moscow) In today's Soviet Air Force exercise of transporting troops and munitions, there were 18 cannons, 150 machine guns, and 1,200 soldiers, which were transported via parachute behind enemy lines in 8 minutes, setting a world record. (9th National Telegram)

U.S. Detains Two More Japanese: A Man and a Woman Photographed an Arsenal

Davenport, USA - Today, a Japanese man, age 29, and a Japanese woman, age 22, were found on a hilltop on the Iowa side of the Mississippi River, overlooking the arsenal, secretly taking photographs. Federal officials, who were already investigating the photographing of Rock Island Arsenal, received a telephone report and immediately went up the mountain to arrest the two Japanese individuals. They confiscated the Japanese man's camera and handed it over to the arsenal authorities. The Japanese individuals claimed they were only taking pictures of ships. The film is currently being developed, and if the arsenal is not included, the Japanese individuals will be released. (9th National Telegram)

Australia's Huge Military Expenditure: £8,800,900 - Unprecedented in Australian History

Canberra - Australian Treasurer Casey presented the Commonwealth of Australia's budget to the House of Representatives today, in which the size of the defense expenditure is unprecedented in Australian history. According to Casey, the total defense expenditure reaches £8,800,900, an increase of £1,792,000 compared to the previous year. According to this budget, the revenue is £81,550,000, and the expenditure is £81,500,500, leaving a surplus of £45,000. Casey also stated that tax reductions amount to £5,275,000. (10th Reuters Telegram)

Arita's Remarks in the U.S.: Discussing Various Issues in Sino-Japanese Negotiations, No Political Ambitions Towards the Philippines

San Francisco - Former Japanese Foreign Minister Kenzō Arita attended the Pacific Society and returned home, passing through here. It is said that Japan will compete in trade in the Philippines and will do so fairly. Japan values trade in all parts of the world, and the Philippines is no exception. However, the Japanese have no political ambitions towards the Philippines. What we hope for is only the development of legitimate trade. Regarding the naval issue, Arita declared that Japan has no intention of engaging in naval competition. Japan's current naval plan is based on the principle of non-threatening and non-aggressive. The Japanese government is eager to begin negotiations with China to resolve the outstanding issues between the two countries, but whether we can succeed depends on the situation at the time of the negotiations and China's willingness to cooperate. (9th National Telegram)

Amidst Internal and External Troubles: French Capital Flees, British Equalization Fund Strenuously Maintains

(London) The British Equalization Fund again made strenuous efforts this morning to maintain the value of the French franc. After the franc's price fell to 76.85, it gradually returned to 76.79. However, the forward price remains weak, proving that the panic among genuine traders has not diminished. These people are desperately seeking self-preservation and are willing to bear a heavy interest rate of 24% per annum. French Premier Blum's failure to reach an agreement with Durães on the Spanish issue makes the life of his cabinet even more precarious than yesterday. Therefore, bold French capitalists are doing their utmost to move capital abroad to prevent the government from implementing a ban on cash exports. The general public now increasingly believes that a united national government that implements a ban on capital flight will be even weaker than the current government. As a result, the Bank of England's intake of French deposits has been increasing day by day. (9th Reuters Telegram)

(New York) French gold worth US$8,365,000 arrived here today, bringing the total gold arriving this week to US$17,373,000, of which US$350,000 came from India and US$2,085,000 came from Colombia. (9th National Telegram)

(London) The Swiss National Bank reduced its interest rate from 2.5% to 2%, which is unrelated to the current situation of the gold bloc currencies. However, it is intended to loosen finances in Switzerland to raise funds for rearmament. It is reported that the discussed national defense funding will issue domestic bonds with an interest rate of around 2.75% for 235,000,000 Swiss francs, raising 80,000,000 francs. (9th Reuters Telegram)

British and French Labor Circles Decide on United Front: Sympathy for the Spanish Government, Not Demanding of Their Own Governments

(London) The General Council of the British Trades Union Congress, the Executive Committee of the Labour Party, and the Parliamentary Labour Party held a joint meeting in Plymouth today, deciding to support the non-intervention policy in Spain. This was decided by a vote after heated debate. Labour MPs Hicks and Dalton also reported on this decision after their trip to Paris. (9th Reuters Telegram)

(Paris) The decision of French labor unions to support the current government has considerably strengthened the position of French Premier Blum. The above decision was made at the closing of the General Confederation of Labour today. In addition to reiterating its full support for the Popular Front government, the Confederation also called on British labor unions to make similar contacts with their government. (9th Reuters Telegram)

(Paris) The Executive Committee of the United General Confederation of Labour held a meeting this afternoon, at which the following resolutions were passed. (1) Germany and Portugal have recently successively submitted reservations regarding the non-intervention in the Spanish civil war, so that genuine non-intervention cannot be implemented. The French government should consult with other democratic governments to reconsider the policies adopted regarding the situation in Spain. (2) The French government must urge the Executive Council of the League of Nations to convene as soon as possible in order to request the Executive Council to strictly implement the Covenant of the League of Nations. (3) British trade unions should make the same request to their government. (4) All members of the United General Confederation of Labour should donate a minimum of one hour's work wage per person to help the wives and children of Spanish Popular Front members who have taken refuge in France. If any employer violates the work contract signed by both labor and management, it has violated the social laws promulgated by the government. The United General Confederation of Labour hereby protests and requests the government to take effective measures to force the employers to comply with the law. (9th Havas Telegram)

(Paris) This afternoon, representatives of the left-wing parties in the Chamber of Deputies held a meeting. The Secretary-General of the Communist Party, Thorez, made a declaration to the meeting, stating that the Communist Party has not changed its original opinion regarding the necessity of providing material assistance to the Spanish government. However, the Communist Party continues to support the general policies of the government. If a motion of censure is proposed at the next reopening of the parliament, the Communist Party will still vote in favor of the government. In short, the Communist Party does not want to make things difficult for the government, but it hopes to reserve the freedom to judge on issues not included in the Popular Front platform. It is reported that the delegation of left-wing parties is an organization composed of representatives of the parliamentary groups of the parties participating in the Popular Front, and its purpose is to coordinate the claims and actions of the left-wing parties in the Chamber of Deputies. (9th Havas Telegram)

(Paris) The Secretary-General of the Communist Party, Thorez, recently sent a letter to the Administrative Committee of the Socialist Party, proposing that the Socialist Party and the Communist Party jointly elect a delegation to visit Premier Léon Blum to ask him to revoke the "blockade policy that is detrimental to the Spanish Republic." He also proposed that the Socialist-Communist Party Adjustment Committee should meet in the near future to discuss joint actions between the two parties to assist the Spanish government, oppose the arms race, and prevent the resurgence of the French fascist threat. The Secretary-General of the Socialist Party, Séverac, replied to Thorez in the name of the Administrative Committee of the Socialist Party. In the reply, he accepted the proposal for the Socialist-Communist Party to elect a delegation to visit Premier Léon Blum. As for the proposal made by the Communist Party for the Adjustment Committee of the two parties to meet for discussion, he said that "your intention has now been recorded, and we are extremely satisfied." Finally, Séverac also expressed his hope that the two parties would continue to unite and fight to safeguard the democratic system, oppose fascism, and prevent war. (9th Havas Telegram)

Plymouth, England - The Trades Union Congress, which is currently being held, continued its meeting today, debating the issues of war and diplomacy. Regarding the situation in Spain, it immediately passed two draft resolutions. The first resolution, concerning the issue of war, was unanimously passed by all representatives. The second resolution, concerning the issue of Spain, was also passed by an overwhelming majority (with only seven dissenting votes). The main points of the two resolutions are listed below. The first states, "If the government wishes to mobilize the country's troops or factories in wartime, we, the trade unions, will not provide assistance and will actively resist it." The second states, "The Spanish Civil War was caused by a small number of military officers betraying the republican system and the legitimate government. The Spanish government and the working class are doing their utmost to suppress the rebels. We have the greatest sympathy for them. The peasants, workers, and young volunteers of the country are fighting for freedom and democracy. We can only pay tribute to their bravery. As for the families of the deceased, we are deeply saddened. This congress hereby reiterates that we will strictly monitor whether the recent orders signed by various governments regarding non-intervention in the Spanish Civil War are detrimental to the Spanish government." It is reported that when the congress opened this morning, a representative named Zach proposed an amendment to the second draft resolution, advocating intervention in the Spanish Civil War. The congress rejected it with 2,978,000 votes against 5,000 votes. (10th Havas Telegram)

(London) There was a heated debate on the Spanish issue at the Labor Congress held in Plymouth today, and a resolution was passed praising the bravery of the Spanish workers who sacrificed themselves to maintain freedom and democracy. The most severe measures must be taken to prevent anyone from using international agreements to harm the Spanish government. Now, there is a special responsibility on the British government, which is to ensure that the Portuguese government implements the non-intervention agreement. Sir Walter Citrine, Secretary-General of the two Congresses, pleaded with the Congress to "curb impulsiveness and use brains" in order to support the officially approved non-intervention agreement policy. Citrine also stated that without the current non-intervention agreement, all countries would be transporting munitions to Spain. If any country is still supplying munitions to Spain, it can only be Germany and Italy. The only way to deal with this is to blockade the Spanish coast by sea, or it may lead to military action. Does the British labor movement dare to take this action? Citrine also answered himself, saying that he dare not say for sure. (10th Reuters Telegram)

Lille, France - After 30,000 textile workers in this area announced a strike yesterday, the labor unrest has now spread to textile factories in the suburbs. Contents of the Franco-Syrian Treaty

(Paris) The treaty between Syria and France was signed today with the first word. According to this treaty, Syria can become an independent country in three years. The treaty is the result of many weeks of negotiations and is based on the British-Iraqi treaty as a blueprint. However, according to Exterior Vienot, the British-Iraqi treaty had omissions regarding the protection of Christians and other small ethnic groups. The treaty signed between France and Syria took this point into account. The treaty stipulates a transition period of three years, during which reforms will be gradually implemented in order to terminate France's trusteeship of Syria, so that Syria can join the League of Nations as an independent country. It also stipulates the reduction of the number of French troops in Syria, the organization of a new judicial system, and the adjustment of the status of French people residing in Syria and their property. (9th Reuters Telegram)

German National Socialist Party Congress: Discussion of Cultural Issues, Claiming National Socialism Inherits Humanism, Attacking Democratic, Communist, and Jewish Culture

Nuremberg: The eighth annual congress of the National Socialist Party opened this morning with a ceremony. After the reading of Führer Hitler's address, a meeting was held at 8 PM to discuss cultural issues. Hitler, government ministers, and members of the diplomatic corps were all present. The first speech was given by Rosenberg, director of the National Socialist Party's foreign affairs group, on the development of humanism. He stated that humanism was originally the essence of medieval philosophy but had long been lost. Now, only National Socialism could inherit the tradition of humanism. Hitler then took the stage to deliver an important speech on the cultural tasks in national activities, attacking Jewish culture, democracy, and Bolshevism. The main points are excerpted below. Hitler first stated, "All the great struggles of the world, in essence, are nothing more than the instinct for human preservation and the tendency for national survival. In modern times, all struggles, traced to their origins, are determined by the purpose of some nations to survive." Hitler then recounted "the terrifying history of the French Revolution," saying that the European continent, having been devastated by the revolution, inevitably suffered the ravages of the god of war. Finally, discussing the history of the late 19th century, he said that every period of history produces great prophets. "If a country's prophet is a politician rather than a writer, then its people can be said to have happiness," he said. Hitler then discussed the various conditions that constitute a national society, saying that only by limiting individual freedom can national unity be achieved. He stated, "The world's major powers have been destroyed one after another by democratic politics, because democratic politics inevitably leads to anarchy. One must know that what has been created through hardship and suffering should not be preserved with weakness and mediocrity. There should be no concession to anarchy. The purpose of Bolshevism is to inject Jewish blood into the bodies of the general population. The Spanish people are being slaughtered in large numbers, and the current example serves as clear proof. Moreover, the destructive actions of Judaism in economic life and its destructive actions in cultural arts are inextricably linked." At this point, Hitler asked economic leaders, religious leaders, and cultural leaders of the National Socialist Party to value the effectiveness of authoritarianism, saying, "Without authority, disasters will inevitably arise, and there will inevitably be an abuse of authority." He also said, "In a certain Christian era, there could only be a certain Christian art. In the era of the National Socialist Party, there can only be a National Socialist art." (Havas News Agency, 10th)

Nuremberg: During the opening ceremony of the eighth annual congress of the National Socialist Party, Wagner, the leader of the National Socialist Party in Monk City, read Führer Hitler's speech, recounting the achievements of the National Socialist Party under its rule and the four-year administrative plan. Finally, he also mentioned the issue of Germany's demand for colonies, which has already been reported in summary by this newspaper's previous telegram. Here, we supplement the following section of Hitler's speech regarding the demand for colonies. Hitler stated that Germany's reasons for demanding colonies were nothing more than two: (1) Germany's economic poverty; (2) the necessity of demanding colonies in order to obtain the raw materials necessary for national survival. He also explained that the reason why Germany must sell its products at low prices is nothing more than to absorb foreign currency in order to purchase imports necessary for German industry. Hitler first stated that a Jewish Bolshevik party, citing poverty as a reason, incites world revolution, wanting to burn and destroy human culture. On the contrary, Germany strives peacefully to solve domestic poverty. Moreover, other countries have an average of 15 to 20 times more land per capita than Germany. Can it still be said that there is poverty for every person who possesses land? Other countries mostly possess abundant raw materials and arable land within their borders. Can it still be said that there are economic difficulties? In Germany, on average, 136 people occupy one square kilometer of land. Although the German people rely on their genius and perseverance to make the most of the land within their borders, they cannot achieve self-sufficiency in food. Since Germany relies on foreign supplies due to a lack of food, it has no choice but to export industrial products as much as possible to compensate. All of Germany's imports are indispensable, and food is especially important. Therefore, Germany cannot but try to export industrial products, even if it lowers prices and even disregards its own losses. Foreigners who do not understand Germany's economic situation often criticize Germany for not dumping industrial products at low prices. Moreover, the German people, feeling the lack of major economic activity areas, do not hesitate to lower prices and export industrial products in exchange for the food that Germany lacks. If this still cannot be understood by the world, then it is truly regrettable. Hitler then quoted the remarks of a British politician, saying that Germany need not purchase raw materials, so there is no need to demand colonies. Hitler said that these words are quite similar to the ingenious theory of Queen Marie Antoinette of France. In the past, when the people of Paris asked for bread, the Queen replied, "If you have no bread, why don't you eat cake?" Is the intention of the British politician to have Germany abandon bread and eat cake? Moreover, if Germany had not suffered the humiliation of the 15 years after the war, if the world had allowed postwar Germany to retain its overseas investments and colonies, then Germany's economy would not have been so difficult. Today, Germany's domestic economy has prospered, and the number of unemployed people in Germany has decreased from 6.5 million to only 1 million. So far, no other country has achieved such satisfactory results. Therefore, Germany has the ability to manage colonies. Is this not clear proof? (Havas News Agency, 9th)

Nuremberg: In Führer Hitler's address read at the National Socialist Party Congress this morning, there was a section mentioning the four-year administrative plan, explaining that after the completion of this plan, Germany's required materials could be completely self-sufficient without relying on other countries. Now, we will excerpt and translate the original text of this section as follows: "In the next four years, Germany's required materials can be supplied by the country's chemical and mechanical industries and the country's mines, without continuing to rely on foreign countries. Moreover, after the completion of the rearmament program, a large number of domestic workers will no longer have to do things, and they can be used to implement this industrial construction plan. This is of great benefit to the national economy. As for after the completion of this construction, the country's production undertakings can be increased in many aspects, and domestic commercial circulation will inevitably develop as a result. As a result, exports will inevitably increase. We will use the funds obtained from exports to purchase food and various necessary raw materials as soon as possible. Moreover, Germany will never give up on resolving the issue of colonies, because the German nation's right to survival is no less than that of other countries. In short, the current issue is not about democracy and freedom. At this critical moment, posterity will never blame us for guaranteeing democracy and freedom. What they will blame us for is whether we have rescued the great German nation from the path of political and economic collapse." (Havas News Agency, 9th)

Guangzhou Premier's Revolutionary Commemoration Meeting Chairman Chiang's Speech (Continued from Yesterday)

(Guangzhou) "China has been weak to the extreme. Above, there is perfunctory inaction and embellishment of emptiness. Below, there is ignorance and few can think long-term. A dignified China is looked down upon by the great powers, and a flourishing civilization is despised by foreign races. People with lofty ideals cannot but feel heartbroken. With a population of 400 million and vast lands of tens of thousands of miles, we should rise up with determination and be invincible in the world. However, due to the corruption of the political system, the court sells titles and offices, and the government plunders and exploits the people more violently than tigers and wolves. Bandits are rampant, and famine is rampant, with starving people everywhere. The people cannot live. Alas, how tragic! Now, strong neighbors are surrounding us, watching us like tigers and eagles, coveting the wealth of our Chinese minerals and the abundance of our products. Piecemeal encroachment has already been seen in succession, and the dismemberment and division of the country are truly worrying at present. Alas, how dangerous! People with a sense of responsibility cannot help but cry out loudly to save the people from fire and water and to support the collapsing building, so that our children and grandchildren may be spared from being slaves to other races. Therefore, we have gathered people with lofty ideals to revive China, and we have worked together with virtuous and talented people. I urge all comrades to encourage each other." After reading the declaration and various articles of association of the Revive China Society, we can know that the Premier at that time led a group of martyrs to launch a revolution at the cost of everything in order to overthrow the Manchus and save the 400 million compatriots from deep water and fire, and to revive the nation from humiliation, danger, and destruction. In order to achieve this goal, we must gather a group of people with lofty ideals, establish a common and consistent belief, and agree to abide by the discipline, succeed in a strong revolutionary organization, so that all comrades can unify their will, unite their spirit, concentrate their strength, and obey orders. Under the personal command of the Premier, we will sacrifice and struggle to restore China, establish a republic, implement our doctrine, and complete the revolution. Because of this organization, everyone was able to carry forward the spirit of "sharing life and death and sharing weal and woe" and "succeeding or dying for the cause" in the year of Yimao and launched the first revolution in Guangzhou. The Premier and the martyrs' hard work and difficult struggle should be emulated by our surviving comrades, especially in Guangdong, where the martyrs Lu (Haodong), Cheng (Kuiguang), Zhu (Guiquan), and Qiu (Si) died. How should we work hard to carry on the past and open up the future, and carry it forward? Especially Lu Haodong, the first martyr who sacrificed for the country, the nation, and the doctrine, when he was arrested and imprisoned, no matter how severely the Qing officials tortured him, he was always unwilling to confess a comrade or an organization. In the confession he wrote before calmly dying for the cause, he solemnly expounded the great righteousness of the revolution. Among them, there are a few sentences that our comrades should still firmly believe in, that is, "Only by abolishing the Manchu Qing can we restore the Han nationality. Only by eliminating the traitors can we abolish the Manchu Qing." The situation at that time was really like this. To revive China, we must overthrow the Manchu Qing. To eliminate the Manchu Qing, we must eliminate the traitors. Now, on the one hand, our country is encountering unprecedented national difficulties. On the other hand, the foundation of domestic political and economic construction has not yet been consolidated. At the same time, the general public still lacks a sense of national consciousness and national awareness. Some people are even willing to be traitors and work for the tiger. I don't know that the environment we are in now is still as bad as before, but the dangers we encounter are many times more serious. If our comrades in the party, government, military, and academia, and all compatriots across the country, cannot inherit the revolutionary spirit of the Premier and the martyrs at this time of crisis and survival, if everyone does not distinguish between regions, work together with one heart and one mind, unite sincerely, and struggle together to build the country and revive the nation, then we will not only be ashamed of the Premier and the martyrs, but also our children and grandchildren will be slaves and animals to others when the country is destroyed and the race is exterminated in the future. In this way, we will be the sinners of the country and the nation for all time. Therefore, when we commemorate the Premier's first decision to launch the revolution today, we must especially remember the tragic management and difficult struggle of the Premier and the martyrs for the country and the nation at that time. Everyone should unite in spirit and struggle and sacrifice for the entire country and nation in order to fulfill the responsibilities of our younger comrades. Everyone must also know that since the Premier first initiated the revolution, our Premier has gone through countless hardships and difficulties and spent a lot of effort. Our martyrs have sacrificed countless heads and blood before they were able to overthrow the Manchu Qing, establish the Republic of China, remove obstacles to the revolution, and create the current foundation for the revolution. Now that we have this foundation and a consolidated revolutionary regime, we can freely decide all plans for saving the country and building the country, and we can freely exercise our powers to promote all kinds of work. This is the most rare and good opportunity for our revolutionary nation-building. Now that we have this opportunity, if we still cannot seize the opportunity to develop and thoroughly reform from all aspects of party affairs, politics, military affairs, economy, and education, and strive to build to realize our doctrine and complete the revolution, then if we miss this opportunity, the country will be destroyed and future generations will never get a chance to turn over. Everyone must also know that the reason why the Premier was determined to launch the revolution and overthrow the Manchu Qing was because the Qing court's politics were corrupt, as stated in the declaration of the Revive China Society, "Politics are not reformed, the system is corrupted, the court sells titles and offices, bribery is rampant, the government plunders and exploits the people more violently than tigers and wolves, bandits are rampant, famine is rampant, with starving people everywhere. The people cannot live." Now that we have assumed the entire responsibility of governing and building the country, we must uphold the revolutionary spirit of the Premier and the martyrs and thoroughly eradicate all the bad habits and corrupt phenomena in the current political system, such as corruption, bribery, perfunctory inaction, embellishment of emptiness, ignorance, and forgetting the big picture for the small. We must strive to reform politics, build a clean and capable government, and promote the construction of all aspects of politics, economy, military affairs, education, and culture. We must transform the people into customs, enrich the country and strengthen the military, and complete the great cause of revolutionary nation-building in order to realize the wishes of the Premier and the martyrs and comfort the spirits of the Premier and the martyrs in heaven. If we still cannot promptly develop the revolutionary spirit and strive to complete the revolutionary cause, and we are still as corrupt as the former Qing government, and a kind of昏庸 still leads to "starving people everywhere. The people cannot live," then others will rise up and revolt against us, and we will be the continuation of the亡淸. Therefore, now is the most critical moment for the success or failure of the revolution and the rise and fall of the country. I hope that comrades from all walks of life in the party, government, and military, especially comrades and compatriots in Guangdong, the birthplace of the revolution, will especially know the difficulties of the pioneers in starting their business and the importance of the responsibilities we now shoulder. Everyone must work together with one heart and strive to build Guangdong into a model province of the Three People's Principles in order to consolidate the foundation of the revolution and complete the great cause of reviving the nation. (Central News Agency, 10th)

It is reported that it has been agreed to imitate the British system. A direct tax office will be established in the central government, and direct tax collection committees will be established in each province. Special direct tax collection committees will be established in the six cities of Shanghai, Pingjin, Qingdao, Hankou, and Guangzhou to concentrate the collection power in the central government and achieve the effect of local cooperation. It is also planned that the salary and remuneration income of the second category of civil servants, and the interest income of the third category of government bonds and deposits will be collected by the Central Direct Tax Office, and the rest will be responsible for the collection committees. Ma Yinchu Talks About Active Rural Finance

The Agricultural Development Bureau's plan to commercialize agricultural products and securitize commodities is indeed an important plan to activate rural finance. When someone came to visit, Ma said that the success of our country's monetary policy in less than a year is really amazing. With the initial unification of China's internal affairs and the lack of a foundation for industry and commerce, such success is beyond the expectations of the general economic circles in the central government. The success of China's monetary policy is actually faster than that of the United Kingdom and better than that of the United States. The environment in developed European and American countries is better than that of our country, but the success of monetary policy also takes considerable time and effort. Since the implementation of our country's monetary policy, industry and commerce have recovered, rural areas have been revived, prices have been stabilized, and foreign exchange has been stable. These are all hard evidence of success. Regarding the revision of the Chamber of Commerce Law, Ma said that the draft has not yet reached the Legislative Yuan. His personal opinion is generally sympathetic to changing the organization of trade associations and supports dividing them into three categories: industrial, commercial, and export, and unifying the industrial and commercial industries under the Chamber of Commerce. National Government Decree National Election Should Abide by Guidelines Those Who Do Not Follow the Right Track Should Be Punished According to Law

(Nanjing) The National Government issued a clear decree on the 10th, saying that the government's decision to hold elections for representatives of the National Assembly was originally intended to establish the proper target of civil rights and plant the initial foundation of constitutional government. The relationship is extremely important. The various laws and regulations previously promulgated have stipulated in great detail. However, there must not be any act of violating laws and regulations in the election process. All officials and people should abide by the guidelines, be loyal and unwavering. If they do not follow the right track, once discovered, they will be punished according to law. The various agencies must not abuse hospitality and courtesy to the election candidates and representatives, except for matters that should be handled in accordance with laws and regulations, in order to show strictness and prevent abuses. Therefore, this is a sincere decree, and we hope that everyone will share their public integrity and complete the important government affairs. There are great expectations. This order. (Central News Agency, 10th)

(Nanjing) The National Election Headquarters stated that the election budget for each province has been reviewed and forwarded by the medical institutions, but several provinces and cities have not yet submitted them. Because it concerns the election policy, it cannot be delayed. Therefore, it has sent another telegram to the general supervisors of elections in each province and city to urge them to report in order to review and forward them. (Central News Agency, 10th)

(Nanjing) The Free Professional Groups Representative Election Office previously received a letter from the Central National Medical Center stating that Article 20 of the National Assembly Election Law states that the qualifications of the staff who elect candidates are said to belong to the executive committee, and some are said to belong to the standing committee. How should the regulations be made in order to show uniformity? Please check and follow. The office has formulated two measures: (1) For medical associations whose executive agency adopts a president system or a director system, the executive staff who participate in the election of candidates should be limited to the president and vice president, or the chairman and vice chairman of the board of directors. (2) For medical associations whose executive agency adopts a committee system, the executive staff who participate in the election of candidates should be limited to the standing committee member or standing director or standing staff. If there is no standing committee member, standing director, or standing staff, the executive committee member or director or staff should be limited. A letter was sent to the National Election Headquarters for review and reply. The reply was received, stating that the proposed measures are feasible, and the Western medical doctors' associations all adopt a committee system, and the entire committee exercises the right to elect, which is not restricted by this measure. The office has telegraphed the representative election offices in each province and city to check and follow. (Central News Agency, 10th)

Guangdong Southern Gui Army Enters Huaxian County, County Government and Party Headquarters Move to Meilu, Former 19th Route Army Troops Respond in Southern Guangdong, Gui Army Hastily Builds Defensive Works on Guangxi Border

Guangzhou correspondence: In recent days, amidst voices for peaceful negotiation in Guangxi, military actions by all parties have not ceased. After the Gui Army units led by Weng Zhaoyuan and others entered southern Guangdong Province, they have been continuously purchasing large quantities of salt, kerosene, and general merchandise in Beihai and other places and transporting them to Guangxi. The county magistrates of counties under the jurisdiction of Qin, Lian, Gao, and Lei have all left their posts. However, the Gui Army is making efforts to keep the staff of various agencies working as usual, and fortunately, archives and files have been preserved, preventing their loss. The tax collection agencies are being managed by personnel dispatched by the Gui Army. As for gambling taxes, gambling merchants in Beihai are paying 100 yuan daily to serve as military expenses. Since arriving in southern Guangdong, Weng Zhaokun has been actively establishing relations with all sectors of society, not interfering in various matters, and only recruiting old troops for military organization with great enthusiasm. The Beihai coastline and nearby mountains are extremely busy with the deployment of defensive works. After the county magistrate of Hepu County abandoned his post and fled, the local self-government organization elected a former county councilor, Mr. Lin, as the temporary county magistrate to temporarily manage county affairs. Public security in the Beihai and Hepu areas is still good, but most wealthy people have moved away. At the beginning of the month, Cai Tingkai personally inspected the defense in southern Guangdong, and former troops of the 19th Route Army flocked to join. Wang Zhisheng, director of the Xuwen military reclamation area, has recently recruited a unit of soldiers to join. Since entering Lianjiang, Weng Zhaoyuan's division has been replenishing its forces daily, and its momentum is growing. Subsequently, as there were no troops stationed in Huazhou, a large number of vehicles were hired the day before yesterday afternoon to transport the troops to Huaxian County, arriving the next morning. County Magistrate Liang of Huaxian, carrying important county government documents, fled to Meilu City, and personnel from the county party headquarters and other agencies also moved to Meilu one after another, temporarily using the Jianjiang Hotel in the city as a temporary office location. County Magistrate Liang and the two executive committee members of the county party, Mr. Chen, urgently telegraphed the provincial government in Meilu to report the Gui Army's entry into Huaxian County. It is noted that Huaxian is the gateway to Gaozhou and Meilu City in southern Guangdong, and Meilu City is the thoroughfare to Yangjiang. Huaxian is only 72 li from Meilu, a distance that can be reached from morning to evening. From Meilu to Shuidong is also only 60 li, and Shuidong is a large port for going out to sea. If Shuidong is lost, Yangjiang City will be threatened. Therefore, the hearts of the people in Meilu have been agitated in recent days. After the 5th, the headquarters of the 4th Route Army of Guangdong has transferred a brigade of a certain division to Meilu for deployment. Since Weng's division arrived in Huaxian, troops from Guangxi Province have continued to arrive in the areas of Bienan, Bobai, Xingye, and Yongchun on the border between Guangdong and Guangxi, deploying defensive works such as digging trenches and building bunkers, without the slightest relaxation. The river surface of Dahe Jilongzhou in Wuzhou was used by the city defense commander yesterday to conduct water mine demonstrations, and the sound was loud. Although the public was notified in advance, residents who witnessed this situation were worried that war would be imminent. Sandbags and barbed wire fences are spread throughout Wuzhou, creating a grim scene. Outside the city, on Baiyun Mountain, Lion Mountain, and the Butterfly Ridge of Sanjiaozui, construction work is being carried out overnight, and the lights are as bright as day. Large cannons are installed in the bunkers along the Dahe River to control waterway traffic, and water is blocked on both banks of the Dahe River to form ponds for military use. In recent days, although negotiations have been ongoing in Nanning, the Gui Army has not for a moment forgotten to deploy military affairs. (8th)

Various Sections of the Yellow River in Shandong Province Report Emergencies, Luokou Water Level Breaks Highest Record

Jinan Correspondence: The floodwaters from Shaanxi Province are gradually flowing into the sea. The upper reaches of the Yellow River in Shandong Province, at Lisheng Tun, have started to see a drop in the water level to 58 meters. The middle and lower reaches, however, are currently experiencing a surge. The water level at Luokou at 2 p.m. today was 31.05 meters, an increase of 2.2 cun compared to the morning, which is the highest record in three years. Zhang Lianjia, the director of the River Affairs Bureau, upon receiving reports of tight construction conditions in various sections, telegraphed the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission in Kaifeng in alarm. The telegram reads as follows:

(Omissions) In recent days, the river water has risen sharply. The county magistrates of Dong'a and Puyang, the chief of the upstream general section, and the chiefs of the south first, south second, north fourth, and north fifth sections, Yu Qijia et al., have successively telegraphed, stating that the people's embankment in Dong'a, from Niu Tun westward, passing through Wei Shan, Fan Po, Wang Po, etc., is thin and weak, with the rapid flow directly impacting, and conditions becoming increasingly precarious. At the Liuyuan water bend embankment in Puyang County, several dozen li of dangerous works, the entrance to the 31st dam, and the inside of the second protective bank have been scoured by two to three chi. The closing bank of the 32nd dam has also been scoured by two to three chi. At the Sun Lou section of the south first section, the Leikou of the fourth dam, and the stone bank of the ninth protective bank have all been flooded. At the Xinzhuang first dam, the bottom has collapsed for a length of eight chi. At the Yangzhuang section of the south second section, the lower corner of the 16th stone protective bank has been scoured for a length of 1 zhang and 5 chi. The Kai protective bank of the Yangshi Daokou sixth protective bank has been scoured by the surrounding flow. At the Longwang Temple Zhang Xinzhuang dams of the north fourth section, all have been flooded. At the small Gejia third stone dam, Zhao Jia dam, and the upper corner of the 23rd stone dam of the north fifth section, each has been scoured by more than 1 zhang. Moreover, the roots of the 25th and 27th willow dams have also been scoured by eight to nine zhang or more. Having received these reports, in addition to having telegraphed instructions to use willow, stone, and sandbags according to the project conditions and to supervise the soldiers and laborers to be vigilant and patrol all night without any negligence, I am respectfully reporting this matter by telegram. Shandong River Affairs Bureau Director Wang Kairu respectfully kowtows.

Knife-Wielding Bandits Besiege the Third District Office in Datian County, Fujian Province; Cause is Forced Assessment of Donations

Xiamen Correspondence: The folk in Datian County have a secret organization called the "Big Knife Society." This spring, the bandit leader Chen Chengyong led over a thousand members to attack the county seat, but they were defeated by the 26th Brigade of the garrison. Chen was killed by a bullet, and the members scattered, but many lurked in the Taoyuan area of the Third District. On August 28, the Big Knife Society suddenly rose again, gathering over 700 members, each wielding knives and spears, and entered Taoyuan Town, besieging the Third District Office. Stationed in Taoyuan was a company of about 100 men from the newly recruited 11th Security Regiment under Zhang Kewu, who lined up to wait. When they approached, they opened fire. The members retreated and advanced repeatedly, holding out for the whole day, and were eventually defeated by the army. Seventeen bandits were killed and many more were injured. However, although the bandits were defeated, some are still gathering in various villages, which has caused panic among the people, and Tiancheng has suddenly entered a state of martial law. As for the resurgence of the Big Knife Society, it is because Datian is located at the intersection of the north and south of Fujian Province, in the hinterland, with closed transportation and poor land and people. The people's knowledge is particularly ignorant and backward. Recently, due to the management of baojia and the strong-arm team, the expenses are taken from the people at each level from the district to the joint bao and the baojia. In addition, to build roads, establish middle schools, and provide compensation to deceased civil servants, each household should pay a donation of more than one yuan per month. Since Datian has no production at all and the people's livelihood is difficult, it is difficult to cope with each assessment. If the district administrators have no funds, they send teams to urge them. Those who are too poor to pay are also troubled by the army's visits, so in addition to the donation, they must also pay for the food and wages of the visiting soldiers. Moreover, most of those who serve as baojia heads are local gentry or intellectuals, with superior status in the village, and can avoid bearing the burden of various donations themselves. Therefore, all donations are borne by the lower-level poor people, which leads to widespread resentment. Moreover, with bandits harassing everywhere, the people are even more miserable. Members of the Big Knife Society seized the opportunity to promote their主張, which is to oppose assessments and eliminate bandits. Those who follow them will have a day to escape from suffering. Therefore, the simple-minded villagers are easily deceived and blindly follow, and secretly gather, which led to the gathering in Taoyuan to besiege the district office on August 28. (September 9)

Fujian Construction Department to Improve Tea and Porcelain Industries

Fuzhou Correspondence: Tea is the most important special product of Fujian Province. However, in recent years, except for the tea produced in a few western counties (northern Fujian), which still has considerable sales due to its special quality, the black tea products of the northern counties (eastern Fujian) are inferior to Qihong in the country, and it is difficult to compete with the tea of India, Ceylon, Java, and other countries in the world market. As for scented tea, it is also gradually being attacked by foreign tea in the northern provinces of China, and sales are gradually decreasing. In order to improve the tea industry, the Fujian Construction Department established a tea experiment farm in Shekou County, Fu'an County, in 1934 to guide farmers in eastern Fujian to improve tea planting and tea making methods. In 1935, the First Tea Warehouse was established in Taijiang, Fuzhou, to manage export tea. However, at that time, due to the urgency of time and insufficient preparation, the warehouse business was contracted to merchants, and all the accumulated problems were not completely eliminated. In 1936, it was all taken back and reorganized, and the Tea Warehouse Management Office was established in the provincial capital, and the Tea Warehouse Branch was established in Saiqi, Fu'an, and Sandu, Ningde, to centrally manage the tea leaves transported from the eastern Fujian counties with the highest output. The management methods are: (1) Order all tea boats to berth at the wharf, and tea pieces should be directly put into the warehouse as much as possible; (2) Strictly crack down on tea theft; (3) Organize tea transportation, and advance customs duties on behalf of shipping companies; (4) Introduce tea merchants to banks for credit overdrafts with low-interest loans. After this year's reorganization, the tea volume has increased. Last year, the total output of red and green tea in the eastern Fujian counties was more than 156,000 boxes. As of the end of August this year, the output of green tea in the northern provinces reached more than 129,700 boxes, and the output of black tea reached more than 91,100 boxes. Compared with last year, black tea has increased by more than 29,600 boxes, and green tea has increased by more than 33,400 boxes. The industries are booming, which is a good sign for the future of Fujian tea.

Porcelain is also a special product of Fujian Province. Dehua in southern Fujian, Ningde in eastern Fujian, and Minqing in northern Fujian all have production. However, due to the imperfect manufacturing methods, sales have declined day by day. In order to improve the porcelain industry in the province, the Construction Department specially established various research and experimental institutions in important porcelain producing areas of the province last year to handle guidance and improvement affairs. The products produced have been considerably improved. Recently, it was decided to hold a Fujian Porcelain Appraisal Conference in the provincial capital in October this year, and a reference department will be set up to solicit porcelain products produced in various parts of the province, porcelain products collected privately, and various products from foreign provinces and countries, for display and appraisal, to achieve the purpose of improvement. All porcelain producing counties in the province have been ordered by the Construction Department to solicit separately from their respective county governments. Other porcelain manufacturing and sales manufacturers in the provincial capital and porcelain products collected privately have been entrusted to the Provincial National Products Exhibition Hall and the National Products Promotion Association to be widely collected and sent to the Construction Department for counting and receipt before September 20, and delivered for display. During the meeting period, the exhibitors are also allowed to select products to participate in the competition or entrust the appraisal conference to sell them on their behalf. If the porcelain products selected are considered excellent by the appraisal conference, the Construction Department will submit a report to the provincial government to give commendations to show encouragement.

Suzhou: Tragedy Arises from Sibling Quarrel

Ye Genlin, a resident of the seventh household in the seventh jia of the fourth bao of Weiting Town, wife Luo, is a second wife. Ye has a daughter Xing Sheng born to his first wife, 18 years old this year. Luo gave birth to two sons, one 5 years old and one 8 years old. On the 9th of this month, the two sons and daughter had a quarrel over eating corn. Ye sided with his daughter, and Luo sided with her son, causing a major conflict between the couple. At 9 o'clock that night, Luo, extremely angry, threw herself into the river and died. When Ye found out and fished her out, she had already died. In a moment of grief, he also threw himself into the river. No one rescued him at the time. It was not until the morning of the 10th that someone discovered his body and fished it out. He and Luo's body were placed side by side on the shore, and it was a sensation throughout the town.

Li Zhankui Commits Suicide in a Tragedy

Li Zhankui, 56 years old, who used to be a patrol officer in the first district of the Water Public Security Bureau, opened a sesame cake shop outside the Changmenwai Main Street to make a living after being laid off two years ago. However, Li Zhankui was not an expert in this field, and his work was taken over by his nephew Shao Kui. Recently, due to the sluggish business, the losses were quite large, and his nephew Li Shao Kui suddenly left, which caused Li Zhankui to develop the idea of ​​being tired of the world. On the afternoon of the 9th, at about 4 o'clock, he took a sharp blade and stabbed himself twice in the groin, causing serious injuries. He fell in a pool of blood and soon died from his injuries. After the District Prosecutor's Office sent personnel to inspect the body on the 10th, he ordered the coffin to be prepared for burial.

Su-Fu Road Fully Open

The Su-Fu Road Motor Company, which is run by merchants, operates long-distance buses on the Su-Fu Highway. The section from Suzhou to Mudu has long been open to traffic, and the section from Mudu to Shanren Bridge is also about to be completed. It is hoped that it will be open to traffic on Double Ten Festival. The section from Shanren Bridge to Guangfu is under construction and will probably be fully open to traffic in January next year. The Construction Bureau is planning to build a road from Guangfu to Wangting to connect with the Su-Xi Highway so that Suzhou and Wuxi can be directly connected by car.

Changshu: Security Team Destroys Newspaper Office

The Telegraph Daily News Agency in Beijian Bei Qu Lane was suddenly attacked by Zhou Tongzhi, the captain of a detachment of the Changshu Security Brigade, and forty or fifty soldiers at around 7:20 p.m. on the 9th. The entire editorial department and business department of the newspaper were destroyed. Everything, including doors, windows, display shelves, tables, chairs, bowls, and utensils, was intact. At the time of the incident, the soldiers blocked road traffic due to their large number, destroyed telephone machines, beat people they met, and destroyed things they saw, causing serious injuries to the newspaper's editorial staff members Shen Timin, Pang Maizhou, Ge Manying, and Xu Yuanru, who were covered in blood. Although the soldiers did not carry guns, they carried bayonets, iron rulers, wooden sticks, and other weapons, and some even rushed into the restaurant opposite to take out long benches to use as weapons, resulting in huge losses. The four injured people were sent to the county hospital. One side reported to the Public Security Bureau for investigation, but County Magistrate Chen Fu, who also served as the brigade commander, was in the province and could not handle the matter that night, allowing the riotous soldiers to play the flute and leave in formation. That night, the newspaper was unable to work due to the chaos of the miscellaneous items, and publication was temporarily suspended the next morning. At this moment, other newspapers in this area, such as the Xinsheng Daily, Qin Daily, Meiri Xinwen, Yi Daily, Chao Daily, and Social Life, held an emergency meeting on the morning of the 10th to first request the Second District Security Command to send personnel to investigate and deal with the matter seriously. As for the cause of the riot by the security soldiers, it was because the newspaper published an article on the 7th entitled "Protecting Prostitutes," which involved the soldiers. After negotiations and corrections, they were still dissatisfied, which led to this action.

Zhang Yulin, director of the local Construction Bureau, originally planned to widen the streets from Guanggiao Bridge to Shengxiang Bridge, from Shengxiang Bridge to the North City Gate, and from North Diao Bridge to Lianrong Bridge, and to demolish the Yuecheng outside the North Gate. The plan was incorporated into the construction plan for 1936 and submitted to the Construction Committee for discussion. At that time, due to the construction of rural roads and the issuance of land prices, the expenses were large, and the original construction funds were insufficient, so it was decided to postpone it. A few representatives were elected to meet with Director Zhang and requested to start the work to improve the appearance of the city and benefit commercial transportation.

New Developments in Abortion Case

Xu Yuanzhen, the eldest daughter of Xu Shaotang, the owner of the old Xu Erquan basket sieve wine bag shop at No. 24 Dashiqiao Street in the city, died suddenly on the afternoon of the 31st of last month. According to her family, Yuanzhen committed suicide by taking poison, but outsiders mostly said that she was killed. Later, after the court appointed an investigating police officer to go to the scene with Shen, the examining officer, to inspect the body, it was found that Yuanzhen's abdomen was swollen and her vagina was bleeding. According to the report of the Shen examiner, the result of the examination was that she died of poisoning, but Qian Chengjun, the chief prosecutor, found that Xu Yuanzhen's death had the suspicion of abortion, so he filed a complaint according to law. Yesterday, he ordered the deceased's mother, Xu Wang, to be summoned for interrogation, which lasted for a long time, and ordered her to be sent back. At the same time, he strictly investigated the midwife who performed the abortion for Xu Yuanzhen and other details for review and handling.

Hangzhou: Extension of Repayment Period for Industrial Revitalization Loan

The Zhejiang Department of Finance had borrowed 720,000 yuan from the China, Jiaotong, Xingye, Yanye, and Continental Banks in Hangzhou last year for industrial revitalization, with a term of one year, and the collateral was Zhejiang local public bonds. Now that the repayment period is approaching, the Department of Finance has negotiated with the lending banks to extend the repayment period by six months, and the collateral will be replaced with 1,496,000 yuan of newly issued second-class public bonds. The monthly interest rate remains at one point.

Arctic Ocean: The Success of an Uninterrupted 10,000-Kilometer Flight (Part 1)

— Translated by Mai Yi

Amidst cloud-covered skies, incessant wind and rain, and the obstructions of ice and snow, the heroic Soviet aviators Chkalov, Baidukov, and Belyakov finally completed their uninterrupted 10,000-kilometer long-distance flight across the Arctic region. The aircraft, a Soviet-made "An125," took off on July 20th from an airfield near Moscow, passing over the Barents Sea, Franz Josef Land, Severnaya Zemlya, and 　Ruba Valoske in Kamchatka, and landed near Nikolaevsk (i.e., Temple Street) at around 1:45 PM on the 23rd. The total distance was three thousand seven hundred and four kilometers. The difficulties encountered along the way were truly insurmountable. Chkalov's account of the flight is very moving, and is translated below:

As I reflect on the entire course of our flight, the first thing I remember is the surge of courage the moment we departed from the airfield near Moscow.

Everything was ready. We were sitting in the cockpit, the engine whirring. Stoman, the engineer who oversaw the construction of the "An125," raised his hand to signal that we should take off. I turned back in the cockpit and signaled to Baidukov and Belyakov:

"Is everything alright?"

"Everything's alright."

I opened the throttle, and the plane began to slide forward, speeding along the cement runway. A large crowd of well-wishers stood in the center of the two-kilometer-long path. The plane's speed increased, leaving them behind. I waved to them, watching them wriggle and turn. But no one could accurately predict when the plane would leave the ground, except for Tupolyev, who stood in exactly the right spot – right where the plane lifted off from the earth. I saw Tupolyev and waved to him.

After making a small circle, I turned the nose of the plane northward. I piloted for the first few hours of the flight. As I steered, I said to Belyakov:

"Sleep, conserve your energy."

But who could sleep when we had just started flying like this! The excitement of the departure made it impossible for my friend to close his eyes.

The plane entered the clouds, constantly heading north. As we reached higher altitudes, the clouds became denser, but we flew higher and higher. After about nine hours, we reached the Barents Sea.

We were over the sea, soaring through a relatively clear gap in the clouds, and we could clearly see small, broken pieces of ice floes in the sea. Here, we increased our altitude even further… thirty meters, three thousand five hundred meters, continuing forward through the clouds. Now, Baidukov took over piloting. Oh, I can’t describe it! I replaced Baidukov before reaching Victoria Island, and at that time, I gave him an order:

"You must sleep, you must, Baidukov."

I continued to pilot the plane northward as before. After some distance, Rivikov told me that we should change direction – we had to turn towards Franz Josef Land. We had already been flying for ten hours. Unexpectedly, the clouds suddenly dispersed, and I saw the land beneath the plane. I couldn't help but shout to my companions:

"Franz Josef Land! Look, Franz Josef Land is here!"

We took photos. The solemnity and beauty of Franz Josef Land truly amazed us; this tranquil natural scene – the great Arctic – certainly aroused a lot of interest in us. We surveyed the area for a long time until the fog obscured our vision.

Next, we flew towards Severnaya Zemlya. Before reaching this place, I asked Baidukov to take over piloting; I decided to rest. I slept on top of the oil tank, covered with a leather sleeping mat, intending to sleep soundly. But the weather was very cold, and I couldn't sleep deeply, only dozing off.

When I got up and looked around, it was raining, and the sky was covered with thick clouds. We had clouds above us, and we had clouds below us! Thus, we could only rely on experience for blind flight. The excellent pilot Baidukov was simply groping in the dark, but surprisingly, he still handled it very skillfully. On the morning of July 21st, we reached Severnaya Zemlya. We always wandered at 80 degrees North latitude. We were fortunate to catch a glimpse of the outlines of several islands through the only gaps in the clouds. Later, we flew towards the mainland, the nose of the plane pointing towards Notvik and Tiksi Bay. The weather conditions were very bad. We struggled through thick, dense clouds and fierce cyclones before reaching Khatanga Bay.

From here, we flew to the Olenek River, then to the Lena River, and after crossing the Lena River, turned towards Tiksi Bay. About sixteen to twenty kilometers away from Tiksi Bay, we changed course to fly to Petropavlovsk in Kamchatka, crossing many mountain ranges of Yakutsk.

We were flying at an altitude of four thousand to four thousand seven hundred meters. The atmosphere gradually thinned, making breathing difficult in the high altitude. However, we still didn't put on our oxygen masks because we calculated that the oxygen we carried was only enough for six hours of flight. We had to save it until flying on the route from Petropavlovsk to the mainland across the Sea of Okhotsk.
