Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

What Exactly is the Inspection Office?

— I

Clearly an organization that protects smuggling

Regarding the establishment of an inspection office by the Hebei-Chahar authorities, it was reported that after private goods in North China were inspected by the inspection office, they would only be subject to a consumption tax of one-eighth of the customs duty, and then they could be freely transported and sold in Hebei, Chahar, Tianjin, etc., without being considered private goods. After this news spread, the whole country was in an uproar and greatly shocked, believing that this system completely destroyed China's customs barrier and maintained a smuggling organization, letters and telegrams flew, and they questioned the Hebei-Chahar authorities about the truth.

The Hebei-Chahar authorities had no choice but to announce the reason for the establishment of the inspection office to the news reporters the other day. Their words were humorous and evasive, a series of excuses. They said that the task of the office was to investigate private goods. All private goods transported and sold within Hebei, Chahar, and Tianjin would be subject to an inspection fee and released, but not taxed. Those transported out of Hebei, Chahar, etc., would still be considered private goods. According to what the Hebei-Chahar authorities announced, after private goods in North China were inspected by the office, those sold in Hebei, Chahar, and Tianjin would not be considered private goods, and only those sold outside of Hebei, Chahar, and Tianjin would be considered private goods. I don't know why there is such a serious distinction between the Hebei-Chahar-Tianjin area and the non-Hebei-Chahar-Tianjin area? That is the first strange thing.

They also said that the inspection fee was not the same as collecting customs duties, but customs revenue is a major lifeline of the national economy. Foreign goods imported into China should pay taxes according to regulations. Why does the office only charge inspection fees for private goods that have not been taxed and allow them to be freely transported and sold? Such private goods should be confiscated and confiscated, which is the proper way. However, the office not only does not detain them, but also inspects and releases them. Once inspected, private goods become official goods, and everything is unimpeded. This kind of organization is clearly a smuggling protection organization. That is the second strange thing.

They also said that they can be freely transported and sold in Hebei, Chahar, and Tianjin, but those transported out of Hebei, Chahar, and Tianjin are still private goods. This treats Hebei, Chahar, and Tianjin as another world, another organization, completely unlike an area under the rule of China's central government. May I ask, what country's land is Hebei, Chahar, and Tianjin? What country's people? What country's politics? Since the puppet organization appeared, the land of several provinces outside the pass has existed in name only. Since the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee appeared, the land in the North China region is also unclear and cannot be investigated. That is the third strange thing.

The Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee is China's Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee. The members of the committee are all dispatched by the central government and appointed by the central government. The committee should be ruled by the central government and abide by China's laws. However, the statements it announces are completely unlike the statements of central government officials, but completely like the statements of a special organization. If this kind of organization is not fundamentally corrected, it will be tested in the areas outside the pass, and it will also be tested in North China. If it is promoted further in the future, I don't know what kind of country China will become, what kind of nation, and what kind of politics.

However, this measure has not satisfied the desires of ambitious people. Now, ambitious countries are singing loudly about adjusting Sino-Japanese relations and about clarifying North China. Then, in the current obscure and unclear situation, with the abnormally developing organization, there may be further changes and unpredictable crises. If I retreat one step, people will advance a hundred steps! If I retreat ten steps, people will advance a thousand steps. It is true that China's land has an end, but people's desires are insatiable. Those who bear the weight of the country should not think of this!

School Starts

— Shen Jiaqian

"The old woman runs a bank? Shameless!" She slapped the dazed Fusheng: "If you have the guts, get steady, what's the point of this stupid boy studying, put him in the shop to learn business. Dreaming with your eyes open, preparing to be the top scorer in the imperial examination?"

Fusheng stroked his burning face and looked at his father. His father just slowly retreated backward, crossing the counter, and only then opened his mouth as if he had something to protect him:

"Of course, you should study. After opening a cigarette and silver shop for a lifetime, I haven't seen a single penny (money), the child will be next year..." Liu Caifu couldn't remember that difficult name for a moment, so he asked Fusheng: "Isn't it next year...

Fusheng looked at his mother's face, and he guarded against the second slap, saying so softly: "Graduating next year."

"Isn't it? He's graduating next year. This child has never been held back a grade. It's better to graduate than to do business. These few coins have to be used."

The boss spoke, supporting himself on the counter with both hands in a protective posture, looking at Fusheng again, who was pitifully standing on one side. The boss's wife heard "graduate," and she didn't know what graduation was, but graduating from a Western school probably had some benefits, so she looked at the kerosene bill to calculate this tuition fee:

"How much money do you need? Let's see what this stupid boy graduates into?"

The boss was happy then. "Fusheng, you tell me, how much money do you need?" Fusheng read the note again, tuition twelve yuan, book fee four yuan, library fee one yuan, a total of seventeen yuan.

The customer shook his head, took back the two cents, and left.

The boss's wife spat a mouthful of phlegm, "Damn! As if they can afford to smoke ×× brand." Grumbling, she walked into the inner room of the shop.

The boss deliberately said loudly to his son:

"Fusheng, after you eat, you watch the shop. I'm going to Beihai to wholesale cigarettes."

Naturally, he was thinking, "Women don't understand things!"

Let's Go Eat!

— Sheli

——One of Travel Notes——

——Guest! Let's go eat!

——Let's go eat! Let's go eat!

In my dream, I was suddenly awakened by this sound. I opened my eyes, the sun had just appeared, it was still early.

Here, is a broken building, two shops across from each other. Don't dislike the dirtiness, in this small hotel, this is considered a special room. In the big house outside, there are beds everywhere, and bedbugs can fight on the straw mats at will, that is the pigsty.

Downstairs is a restaurant, selling rice, 粥 (congee), all kinds of noodles, but the side dishes are only cheap goods; none of the customers here can afford a dish that costs two dimes.

Although the town is small, because this is the main road into the city, there are many people coming and going. There are several shops on the street selling "home-style meals" and offering lodging for traveling merchants.

It seems like fate, last night's wind and rain still kept me here.

I didn't expect that in this quiet small town, these noisy sounds would ring out so early in the morning.

I got up resentfully, leaning on the windowsill and looking down at the street;

On the street: several country people walked by hurriedly. In the restaurants, this one, that one, the boss, the waiter, all crowded at the door, waving to those country people, opening their mouths, shouting:

——Guests, let's go eat——

——Order some rice before you leave——

The landlady downstairs from us was also smiling hard, shouting loudly.

Those country people seemed a little timid, lowering their heads and walking straight on.

The street temporarily quieted down.

However, when I went downstairs to wash my face, suddenly the noisy sound flew up again. The landlady, holding a washbasin, hurriedly put the washbasin in front of me and rushed to the door. Immediately I heard her voice. I turned my head: three figures had just flashed past the door.

The landlady's voice stopped, with disappointment on her face.

——What's the point of shouting? If people want to eat, they will eat; if they don't eat, it's no use shouting until your throat is broken!

I don't sympathize with her disappointment. I think it's stupid to use this kind of slogan-like method to attract customers.

She glanced at me and walked towards me:

——Guest! You don't know, in the past, country people coming to the city always rested here and ate something, but in recent years, things are not right. If you shout, they are still unwilling to come. If you don't shout, even less people will come. Country people are very bad!

——It's not their fault, the times are bad, where do country people get the money to eat?

The waiter interjected from the side.

I didn't say anything. I think the waiter's words are right, and the landlady's shouting is using aural temptation, which is not wrong in the business world. Many shops in the city also have their waiters wear paper hats and stand at the door shouting during auctions; it's a pity that this kind of temptation has lost its effect in the current "bad times."

Just as I was thinking this, the voices became noisy again:

——Let's go eat!

——Let's go eat!

It is a double cry of hunger!

The Authority of God

— Rui Zhi

——Random Notes from Mountain Living——

Coming to live in the mountains and forests, this is the second time in my life.

On a sweltering afternoon, a friend asked me to go to his hometown. He said, "People only know to go to famous mountains like Qingwu to escape the summer heat, but my hometown also has mountains and rivers and large forests. It doesn't cost much money, and it's quieter than famous summer resorts. It should be a good place for us poor scholars!" Hearing what my friend said, I finally left the stuffy and noisy metropolis that evening and came to this quiet and beautiful mountain.

In the city, I was stuck sitting in that attic above ninety degrees every day. It seemed like I was tired and without energy all day long. But when I got here, everything changed. The beauty of nature's scenery, the lives and laughter of the mountain people, all transformed me, who was trapped in the city like a little crow, into an energetic wild cat.

The summer countryside is lovely. At daybreak, birds are chirping on the eaves. The face of the rising sun, like an egg yolk, rises behind the mountain slope. It doesn't make people feel disgusted at all. Its light shines on the fields in the valley. Every ray of golden light glitters like countless golden rivers. The farmers, carrying their farm tools or riding on the backs of oxen, sing ditties and mountain songs, beginning their work in the golden sunlight. In the afternoon, the sun climbs to the treetops. The old banyan trees, which require both arms to encircle, cast patches of shade. Sitting and chatting, gazing at the green of the distant mountains and the turquoise streams, a cool breeze blows. The scorching sun in the mid-sky seems to have lost its authority, as lovely as the winter sun. The village children riding on the backs of oxen are as elegant as in famous paintings, stirring the remaining golden water waves in the mountain stream. The earth is silent, only the soft sound of leaves playing a lullaby for the afternoon nap.

At midnight, the moon leaps out from the black shadows of the distant mountains. A line of snow-white silver light shoots into the gauze window. Gazing at the wilderness, the forests are all white. The shadows of the trees in front of the window move, and the moonlight seems to be undulating in the water, sometimes bright, sometimes dark. A gentle breeze blows, and the fields seem to be filled with countless lovers whispering. Fireflies fly by, like shooting stars streaking across the sky. (To be continued)

Suzhou Storytelling

Cao Xiaoying's Jade Dragonfly

Zhongxi (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening: "Pipa of Xunyang"

Sima Xiangshan, Jiangzhou. Anchored at the ancient ferry of Xunyang at night. Seeing off guests sadly, sharing farewell. Reed flowers and maple leaves in the autumn evening of the river. Thinking that I am, lamenting the official life, drifting like duckweed. A farewell banquet held as the sail is raised on the water. Gazing at the moon in the center of the river, the sound of drums has reached the second watch. Suddenly, the sound of lamentations rises on all sides, tuning the strings. Asking where, the sorrowful sound is like a complaint. Therefore, the host and guests approach the neighboring boat. Asking her to come closer, she appears half shy. Seeing her, Aunt Qiu is still graceful, adding a cup of wine to the table. Listening to her, recounting her life, filled with old dreams. Alas, spring flowers and autumn moon do not remain. The phoenix strings follow the tune of the silver plectrum. Who knows, the mandarin duck curtains are empty, longing for the fallen jade hook. Past events are unbearable to look back on. Countless unspeakable words are told from the beginning. Seeing her, the remaining rouge and powder are only regrets. Blood-stained skirt of old pomegranate color. Later, the carriages and horses gradually thinned, sadly desolate. How could she marry the floating Liang husband and leave? Just like, autumn wind abandons the palace silk fan. The crescent moon is hard to repair with the jade axe. Knowing that, from ancient times, the pleasure ground is like the official sea. Changes in the world go on and on. I am also, a drifting traveler like you. At the end of the road, sympathetic tears meet. But, the pipa of Xunyang has a thousand years of hatred. I advise you, play another song, what more can you ask? It's just that, I have nothing to give you as a gift, so I turn it into a new melody and offer it as a song. When the song ends, the wine is gone, and people leave, a sound is heard from the returning horses. I feel that, red powder and blue shirt, tears flow together.

Xing Ruiting's Three Smiles

Shanghai (1100) 4:00 PM to 4:30 PM Opening: "Guan Shoufeng's Night Exploration of the Tiger's Den"

The affairs of the world are like a game of chess, weighed on a scale. The changes of the wind and clouds stir up dust. Since ancient times, how many infatuated people have there been. After experiencing the vicissitudes of life, feeling the past and present. Thinking that I am, a chivalrous heart and proud bones. Ten years of wandering the rivers and lakes. Lamenting my own life as a mayfly, accustomed to being in the world, not fair. Jia Shu's public love has changed to joy. Full of love and affection. Before leaving, he entrusted the important love affairs. I should keep a little of my heart. Who knows that Fengxi is a flower bud envied by wind and rain. Who will come to protect the flower bell. Only regret that, mistakenly entering the tiger's den, her beautiful face is imprisoned. Spring locks the heavy door, and no one is seen. Allowing her to drop tears and cry like a cuckoo in the night moon. The embroidered curtains are lonely, weeping in the twilight. Fortunately, the secret message is passed by the mother. Suddenly touching the hero's listening ears. So, risking his life to explore the tiger's den. There is a wall to listen to, an ear close to the wall. Secretly looking at, the general has not changed his slave state. From time to time, he begs for a beauty with a flattering face. Moreover, strings of pearls and rare treasures are dazzling. Yaqin is entrusted to mediate. Unexpectedly, the daughter has changed her love to golden objects. She only values gold, not love. Since ancient times, the field of love has been full of changes. Gold can buy a beautiful woman's heart. Knowing that, the mirror is a flower in the water and the moon in the mirror, empty into a shadow. Regretting that, suspecting rain and cloud, pretending to be true. But I, witnessing the situation, often sigh. It is difficult to suppress the tide of anger for a while. I can't wait to cut off this kind of love for you. Don't fail the deep trust of that year. Alas, the son's infatuation is like a dream, sadly becoming a consequence that changes the cause. Therefore, a letter is sent quickly, telling him to say goodbye to his parents and set off. Just as well...

Zhang Yunting's Jade Dragonfly

Dunben (800) 9:05 PM to 10:00 PM

Opening: "National Flower"

Although the plum blossom is not the king of flowers. Its character is pure and outstanding. Since ancient times, poets have praised it. The fame of the flower queen is unparalleled in the world. The chrysanthemum is a recluse among flowers. The lotus is also worthy of a gentleman. Zhou Zi loved lotus, and Tao loved chrysanthemum. The interests of the two are very unusual. Don't know, the plum blossom combines reclusive and gentlemanly qualities. Its nature is gentle, its character is high, and its appearance is dignified. People in the world often praise peaches and plums. Peach blossoms are gorgeous, and plum blossoms are fragrant. That plum blossom only settles in peace. Unwilling to follow the fashion and learn new makeup. The beauty of the world is unrestrained and vulgar. Ashamed to compete with peaches and plums for fragrance. Without a good matchmaker, what harm is there? The fairy of Miaogu has no lover. Friends in the mountains are pine and bamboo. The night is clear wind, the moon and frost. Those ordinary flowers only listen to orders. Who can occupy the spring first? So it is said that the new moon unfolds its eyebrows and the stars shine. The old plum opens its mouth, and hundreds of flowers are busy. Who knows the ancient times? Only to say that the eyes of the world are blind. But unexpectedly, there is still Lin Hejing with affection. To say about the voice of Meng Xiangyang. And now the national flower is determined to be more glorious.

Zhou Zhenyi's Demon Biography

Yuanchang (1120) 12:45 AM to 1:30 AM

"Pearl Pagoda's Boudoir Complaint" (Mimi Collection Inaugural Issue)

A wanderer far away from home seeks relatives. Coincidentally, he meets Chen Lian, who has resigned, celebrating his birthday. At fifty, without a son, he laments Bo Dao. Zhonglang and Yue Nu are pitiful. The sound of pipes and drums adds to the grief and sorrow. It is rare for Da Ruan to come from a thousand miles away. The crowns and hats are like the gatherings of officials. Therefore, the inner hall conveys the message to see the madam. The madam's face is as cold as ice. A few words do not make ice charcoal. Her proud bones are like flowers facing up. She will never pass the examination, never enter the door. Alerted, the maid Cui Ping behind the screen is concerned. A soft and clever heart. Talking to herself, groaning, ascending to the boudoir to tell the female monarch. Saying that the madam was alarmed at first, then angry, and finally laughed coldly a couple of times. I hope you can correct your loving mother's faults. Repay the kindness of your aunt in those years. A close relative mediates well. Qianjin is at a loss when she hears the words. Movies

Star Information

A party to entertain all walks of life is currently being actively prepared. On the vast square of the Fenglin Bridge Main Factory, many colored buildings are being built, similar to the memorial archways at the West Lake Exposition, designed by Wan Guchan.

The Screenwriting Committee has recently established the Star Library, ordering various central drama and film books and newspapers, and major bookstores have donated books and newspapers, especially the Tianma Bookstore, which has given various series of books.

The main factory's "Women's Rights," "Night Party," "Eternal Smile," and the Alber Road Second Factory's "Loyal Hearts in Life and Death" and "Qingming Season" are being actively filmed these days and will be completed around the Mid-Autumn Festival.

On the vast open-air photography field, there is now a very beautiful garden, dance floor, and grape arbor, everything is available. The visit is all for the new construction, in fact, this is the garden hotel scenery in "Night Party."

The shooting field of Factory One has recently been transformed into a magnificent hall, which is the charity dance party of celebrities in "Women's Rights." The vastness of the entire shooting field can be imagined.

Shen Xiling's new work "Crossroads" will be launched after "Loyal Hearts in Life and Death," and most of the leading actors are newcomers.

"Water Music House" Song and Dance Venue

Seeking "Yegor Bulychov"

Yegor Bulychov is an important character in Gorky's posthumous work "Yegor Bulychov and Others." It is very, very difficult to create a character like the one Gorky portrayed. This play is being rehearsed by the Haiyan Drama Troupe. Haiyan is a drama group composed entirely of newcomers, and they have spent four or five months of hardship. No one has ever paid attention to them or supported them. They humbly bury themselves in research everywhere.

Now, they feel that this role in rehearsal is somewhat unsuitable and need to find a more wholesome actor to play it. It has been decided to extend the date of the premiere and to seek another actor to play the role of "Bulychov." He must be tall, fluent in Mandarin, have a loud voice, and slightly wide cheekbones. Anyone who thinks they have such talent, please contact the company at No. 7 Huatongfang, Beixizang Road Bridge, every day from 2 PM to 7 PM.

"Cow Nose" The Third Collection of Blessing Series Will Be Published

Huang Yao's "Cow Nose," the first humorous cartoon book in China, has published the first two collections, which have been selling well both domestically and abroad, reaching more than 20,000 copies. It has won high praise from the United States, Germany, England, Japan, and other countries, which believe that "it brings together the comedic points of the Chinese people to develop pure Chinese rich jokes, introduces China's unique humor, and truly makes people wake up from sleep. Reminiscing at any time and laughing uncontrollably, it is not only interesting and profound but also contains satire. Its style is unique in the international cartoon world, using extremely simple lines. It can draw very lively movements and delicate expressions, which is even more rare. The protagonist's half-nose face and body are organized and very easy to learn. Therefore, both young and old like to imitate and draw, recognizing this cow nose as a representative of Chinese comedy." The first collection has been published in three editions, and the second collection has been republished. They are all published by the China Book Company on Fuzhou Road in this city. Now, the third collection has been compiled with excellent works, and there is also a "Blessing Collection," which is all single-panel satirical paintings, purely performed by Cow Nose, still taking a humorous tone, satirizing all social figures. The cover is printed in four colors, which is even more magnificent. The selling price is still set at 15 cents, and it is currently being compiled and will be published soon.
